25 /**
26  * This Controller handles API Requests concerning events
27  */
28 class EventController @Inject()(cc: ControllerComponents,
29                                 protected val dbConfigProvider: DatabaseConfigProvider,
30                                 val silhouette: Silhouette[AuthEnv],
31                                 val organizerService: OrganizerService,
32                                 val userService: UserService,
33                                 eventService: EventService,
34                                 locationService: LocationService,
35                                 importService: ImportService)
36     (implicit context: ExecutionContext)
37     extends AbstractController(cc)
38     with HasDatabaseConfigProvider[JdbcProfile]
39     with Util {
40 
41   val log = Logger("api.event")
42 
43   def getEvent(id: Long) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
44     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
45 
46     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
47 
48     db.run(q.detailed).flatMap(x => x.headOption match {
49       case Some(r) => {
50         if (!r.location.latitude.isDefined || r.location.latitude == Some(0)) {
51           locationService.geocode(r.location).map(l => Ok(Json.toJson(r.copy(location = l))))
52         } else {
53           Future.successful(Ok(Json.toJson(r)))
54         }
55       }
56       case _ => Future.successful(NotFound)
57     })
58   }
59 
60   def getEventByShortId(id: String) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
61     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
62 
63     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.shortId === id) yield e;
64 
65     db.run(q.detailed).flatMap(x => x.headOption match {
66       case Some(r) => {
67         if (!r.location.latitude.isDefined || r.location.latitude == Some(0)) {
68           locationService.geocode(r.location).map(l => Ok(Json.toJson(r.copy(location = l))))
69         } else {
70           Future.successful(Ok(Json.toJson(r)))
71         }
72       }
73       case _ => Future.successful(NotFound)
74     })
75   }
76 
77   def searchEvents(search: Option[String], location: Option[Long], category: Option[Long],
78                    sort: Option[String], sortDir: Boolean, from: Option[Timestamp], to: Option[Timestamp]) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
79     log.debug("Rest request to search events")
80     
81     val t = event
82       .optionalFilter(search, (s: String,e: EventTable) => upper(e.name) like upper("%" + s + "%"))
83       .optionalFilter(category, (c: Long, e: EventTable) => e.categories.filter(_.id === c).exists)
84       .optionalFilter(location, (l: Long, e: EventTable) => e.locationId === l)
85       .optionalFilter(from, (f: Timestamp, e: EventTable) => e.from >= f)
86       .optionalFilter(to, (t: Timestamp, e: EventTable) => e.from <= t)
87       .filter(e => e.to.getOrElse(plus(e.from,oneDay)) >= currentTimestamp)
88 
89     val s = t.sortColumn(sort,sortDir).queryPaged.detailed
90     
91     returnPaged(s,t,db)
92   }
93 
94   def getNearby(id: Long) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
95     log.debug("Rest request to get events nearby another event")
96 
97     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
98 
99     db.run(q.detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
100       case Some(e) => {
101         val q = EventTable.event.join(LocationTable.location).on(_.locationId === _.id)
102           .sortBy(y => geoDistance(e.location.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, e.location.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, 
103               y._2.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f), y._2.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f)))
104           .map(_._1).filter(y => y.id =!= e.id && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
105         val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
106         returnPaged(s,q,db)
107       }
108       case None => Future(NotFound)
109     }
110   }
111 
112   def getSameViewed(id: Long) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
113     log.debug("Rest request to get events other participants also visit")
114 
115     val q = ParticipantCountView.participantCount.filter(_.id === id.bind)
116       .join(EventTable.event).on(_.event_fk === _.id)
117       .sortBy(y => y._1.count.desc).map(_._2)
118       .filter(y => y.id =!= id.bind && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
119 
120     val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
121 
122     returnPaged(s,q,db)
123   }
124 
125   def deleteEvent(id: Long) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { (request,organizer) =>
126     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
127 
128     val q = event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).delete
129 
130     db.run(q).map {
131       case 0 => NotFound
132       case x => Ok(Json.toJson(x))
133     }
134   }
135 
136   def createEvent() = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
137     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
138       form => {
139         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
140       },
141       data => {
142         log.debug("Rest request to create event")
143 
144         eventService.insertEvent(data, organizer).map {
145           case Some(ev) => Ok(Json.toJson(ev))
146           case None => BadRequest
147         }
148       })
149   }
150 
151   def updateEvent(id: Long) = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
152     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
153       form => {
154         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
155       },
156       data => {
157         log.debug("Rest request to update event")
158 
159         val location = locationService.insertOrGet(data.location)
160 
161         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
162 
163         val catParents = data.categories.filter(_.id.isDefined).map {
164             case cat =>
165               cat.id match {
166                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).flatMap(_.parent).result
167               }
168           }
169 
170         val catSimple = data.categories.filter(_.id.isDefined).map {
171             case cat =>
172               cat.id match {
173                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
174               }
175           }
176         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(catSimple ++ catParents).map(_.flatten.distinct)
177 
178         val eventQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).result.map(_.headOption)
179 
180         db.run(imagesQuery.zip(categoriesQuery).zip(eventQuery)).zip(location).flatMap {
181           case (((images,categories),Some(ev)),Some(location)) => {
182             val event = Event(Some(id), data.name, data.from, data.to,
183                               data.description,
184                               organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1l),
185                               data.priceMin, data.priceMax, ev.shortId)
186 
187             val getQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id)
188 
189             db.run(getQuery.update(event) >> getQuery.result.map(_.head))
190               .map(r => Some((r,images,categories)))
191           }
192           case _ => Future.successful(None)
193         }.flatMap {
194           case Some((event,images,categories)) => {
195             val dropImages = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity.filter(x => x.entityId === id && x.entityType === EntityType.Event).delete
196             val dropCategories = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory.filter(x => x.eventID === id).delete
197             val dropQuery = dropImages.zip(dropCategories)
198 
199             val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1l),event.id.getOrElse(-1l),EntityType.Event, img._2))
200             val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1l),event.id.getOrElse(-1l)))
201             val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1l)).detailed
202             db.run(dropQuery >> imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed).map(x => Some(x))
203           }
204           case None => Future.successful(None)
205         }.map {
206           case Some(e) => Ok(Json.toJson(e))
207           case None => BadRequest
208         }
209       })
210   }
211 
212   def insertCSV = organizerRequest(parse.multipartFormData) { case (request,organizer) =>
213     log.debug("Rest request to insert events by csv")
214 
215     request.body.file("csv").map { case x =>
216       val file = x.ref.path.toFile()
217 
218       eventService.insertCSV(file,organizer)
219      }.map(_.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))).headOption.getOrElse(Future.successful(BadRequest))
220   }
221 
222   def participate(id: Long) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
223     log.debug("Rest request to participate in event")
224 
225     val q = (event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind).result)
226       .zip(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1l).bind).result)
227 
228     db.run(q).map(x => (x._1.headOption,x._2.headOption)).flatMap {
229       case (Some(e),None) => {
230         db.run(ParticipantTable.participant += ((user.id.getOrElse(-1l),id)))
231         Future.successful(Ok)
232       }
233       case (Some(e),Some(p)) => Future.successful(Conflict)
234       case (None,_) => Future.successful(BadRequest)
235     }
236   }
237 
238   def unparticipate(id: Long) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
239     log.debug("Rest request to unparticipate in event")
240 
241     db.run(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1l).bind).delete)
242       .flatMap {
243       case 1 => {
244         Future.successful(Ok)
245       }
246       case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
247     }
248   }
249 
250   def getSliderEvents = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
251     log.debug("Rest request to get events for slider")
252 
253     db.run(SliderEventTable.sliderEvent.sortBy(_.number).flatMap(_.event).detailed).map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))
254   }
255 
256   def importFacebookEvent(url: String) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { case (request,organizer) =>
257     log.debug("Rest request to import event from url")
258 
259     importService.getEvent(url, request.identity)
260       .map(x => x.map(y => Ok(Json.toJson(y))).getOrElse(BadRequest))
261   }
262   
263   def copy(id: Long) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { case (request,organizer) =>
264     log.debug("Rest request to copy event")
265 
266     db.run(EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id && x.creatorId === organizer.id).detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
267       case Some(ev) => {
268         val locationForm = LocationForm.Data(ev.location.id, ev.location.name, ev.location.country,
269                                              ev.location.city, ev.location.street, ev.location.website,
270                                              ev.location.phone, ev.location.comment, ev.location.link, ev.location.zip)
271         val eventForm = EventForm.Data(ev.name, ev.from, ev.to, ev.categories.map(_.category), locationForm, 
272                                   ev.images.map(x => TaggedImageForm.Data(x.id.get, x.tag)), ev.description, ev.priceMin, ev.priceMax)
273         
274         eventService.insertEvent(eventForm, organizer).map {
275           case Some(event) => Ok(Json.toJson(event))
276           case _ => BadRequest
277         }
278       }
279       case None => Future.successful(BadRequest)
280     }
281   }
